  <script>
   /*<![CDATA[*/

        (function () {
            // if (checkIfConsentCookieIsPresent()) {
            //     return;
            // }

            if (checkBypassCookiePresent()) {
                return;
            }

            if (checkIfCookiesAreWritable()) {
                redirectToInterceptionPage();
            } else {
                // Privacy by Default
                return;
            }

            // Help functions
            function checkIfConsentCookieIsPresent () {
                var localTCString = getCookie('euconsent-v2');
                return localTCString && localTCString.length > 0;
            }

            function checkBypassCookiePresent () {
                var bypassCookieValue = getCookie('euconsent-bypass');
                return bypassCookieValue && bypassCookieValue === '1';
            }

            function getCookie (cname) {
                var name = cname + '=';
                var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
                var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');

                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];

                    while (c.charAt(0) === ' ') {
                        c = c.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (c.indexOf(name) === 0) {
                        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                    }
                }
                return '';
            }

            function checkIfCookiesAreWritable () {
                try {
                    // Create cookie
                    document.cookie = 'cookietest=1';
                    var ret = document.cookie.indexOf('cookietest=') !== -1;

                    // Delete cookie
                    document.cookie = 'cookietest=1; expires=Thu, 01-Jan-1970 00:00:01 GMT';
                    return ret;
                } catch (e) {
                    // console.log('cookies are not allowed');
                    return false;
                }
            }

            function redirectToInterceptionPage () {
                var tcfLandingpageURL = window.location.protocol + '//'+ window.location.host + '/consent-management/';
                window.location.href =tcfLandingpageURL;
            }
        })();
    
/*]]>*/
  </script>

   /*<![CDATA[*/

        window.consent = {
            features: {},
            purposes: false,
            tcString: '',
            tcStringVersion: 1.1,
            acString: '',
            full: false
        };

        // Brain tracking is extra because of feature permissions
        try {
            window.__tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function() {
                window.__tcfapi('getPermission', 2, function(valid) {
                    if (valid === null || valid === undefined) {
                        valid = window.PageConfig.optin;
                    }
                    window.consent.features.brainTracking = valid;
                }, 'brainTracking');
            });
        } catch (e) {
            window.consent.features.brainTracking = window.PageConfig.optin;
        }

        // AdService depends on purposes
        try {
            window.__tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function() {
                window.__tcfapi('getTCData', 2, function(tcfObject) {
                    window.consent.purposes = {};
                    window.consent.purposes.publisher = tcfObject.publisher;
                    window.consent.purposes.purpose = tcfObject.purpose;
                    window.consent.purposes.special = {consents: tcfObject.specialFeatureOptins};
                    window.consent.tcString = tcfObject.tcString;
                });
            });
        } catch (e) {}

        try {
            window.__tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function() {
                window.__tcfapi('getACString', 2, function (acString) {
                    window.consent.acString = acString;
                });
            });
        } catch(e) {}

        try {
            window.__tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function() {
                window.__tcfapi('getPermission', 2, function(valid) {
                    if (valid === null || valid === undefined) {
                        valid = false;
                    }
                    window.consent.full = valid;
                }, 'fullConsent');
            });
        } catch(e) {}

        // version
        try {
            window.__tcfapi('getTCFVersion', 2, function(response) {
                if (!response !== null && response !== undefined) {
                    window.consent.tcStringVersion = parseFloat(response);
                }
            },null);
        } catch(e) {}
